  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_17bc4c2c-6786-4f57-8d6a-ecd109d8e28b'

<span id="freeTextContainer11679569995638624946">Mercurial and charming, Tate Larson is a rising author and playboy who has a different woman on his arm every night of the week. Focused on his work, Tate has no plans to settle down any time soon.   <span id="freeText11679569995638624946" style="display:none">Mercurial and charming, Tate Larson is a rising author and playboy who has a different woman on his arm every night of the week. Focused on his work, Tate has no plans to settle down any time soon. That is until he meets his pretty new assistant, Piper Donovan. <br /><br />Desperate to escape the promise of backwater living, Piper ditched her Alabama hometown and never looked back. That was almost two years ago. Now that she is out of a job and her bank account is running on fumes, she’s desperate to find a job, fast. She finds the break she is searching for when she lands a position at Bookish Temptations. A little dancing and a lot of drinks with the girls seem the perfect way to celebrate. After a brief but explosive encounter with a man she was never supposed to see again turns out to be the same man she will be bending over backwards to please, her every instinct tells her to run. But when running means leaving the life she has struggled so hard to create, Piper decides her only option is to continue working for the devastatingly sexy Tate Larson...even if it kills her. <br /><br />Unable to deny their growing attraction, they struggle to keep their distance in a relationship that requires anything but. <br /><br />*This book is intended for mature audiences.*</span>

        $('edition_21758557').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_21758557').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_21758557').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

</script></div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18171632097519558268">HOT DAMN! WHAT A RIDE!!<br/><br/>THIS BOOK WAS SO MUCH FUCKING FUN I FEEL LIKE I NEED TO WRITE THIS REVIEW IN ALL CAPS IN ORDER TO CONVEY MY EXCITEMENT! But I won’t. Because that is annoying and since I will no doubt be annoying you with my incessant gushing over this book and its author, I’ll let that one go.<br/><br/>Now, onto the gushing…<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556534._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First gushing over the author. I have read books by this author before. Some I have loved and some I have loved a little less but one thing has always remained true: it is fuck</span>
  <span id="freeText18171632097519558268" style="display:none">HOT DAMN! WHAT A RIDE!!<br><br>THIS BOOK WAS SO MUCH FUCKING FUN I FEEL LIKE I NEED TO WRITE THIS REVIEW IN ALL CAPS IN ORDER TO CONVEY MY EXCITEMENT! But I won’t. Because that is annoying and since I will no doubt be annoying you with my incessant gushing over this book and its author, I’ll let that one go.<br><br>Now, onto the gushing…<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556534._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First gushing over the author. I have read books by this author before. Some I have loved and some I have loved a little less but one thing has always remained true: it is fucking hard to put her books down. She has a talent for sucking you in and keeping you there until the ending comes all too soon. Whether her books are darker or sexier there is always plenty of humour to be found. Her characters seem so real and their emotions are so well described that you cannot help but love them.<br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556535._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And so gushing over the characters. LOVED THEM!! Tate has a reputation for being a complete and utter jerk but Piper has desperation on her side so she is not about to take any of his shit. The banter and push and pull between these two was intensely enjoyable. I lost count of the amount of times I was snorting at either of their quips or the times my toes curled over because the games they played with each other were just so satisfying. The attraction between them is undeniable, the angst delicious and the sexual tension was tangible.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556536._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which brings us to gushing over the sexy times. Because holy wow, this book was HOT! All that fire and tension and constant back and forth translated into some intense sexy times. All the grabbing, clothes tearing, passionate kissing and wall banging you could ever want are inside these pages and not once does any of it become stale. In fact with the back and forth between these two each time just becomes more and intense.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556537._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now, gushing over all of it. I cannot find a single thing to dislike about this book. It is hot and funny and sweet angsty and sexy and that ending… OMG that ending. Just read it!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467133758i/19556538._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review)<br><br> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1634007669022300586"><br/><b>This book starts out with a serious BANG!</b><br/><br/><img alt='' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424784ra/847038.gif' width='480' height='267' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Piper and Tate have a brief but explosive encounter in the ladies room at a night club. Piper and Tate are virtual strangers and neither ever plans to encounter the other again. Fate has another plan. Piper's new job leads her to her mystery man. She soon discovers the reason he has not been able to keep an assistant for more than a few weeks tops. He is a complete jackass.<br/><br/>Tate is a mercurial writer with a short temper. He is immediately irritated that Pi</span>
  <span id="freeText1634007669022300586" style="display:none"><br><b>This book starts out with a serious BANG!</b><br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424784ra/847038.gif" width="480" height="267" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper and Tate have a brief but explosive encounter in the ladies room at a night club. Piper and Tate are virtual strangers and neither ever plans to encounter the other again. Fate has another plan. Piper's new job leads her to her mystery man. She soon discovers the reason he has not been able to keep an assistant for more than a few weeks tops. He is a complete jackass.<br><br>Tate is a mercurial writer with a short temper. He is immediately irritated that Piper is his assistant. Piper can not believe her luck. Her BAD luck. Tate is incorrigible.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424784i/847039._SY540_.jpg" width="255" height="385" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper is a girl trying to make her way in the city. She is a small town girl from humble beginnings and she is determined to make more of her life. She has been struggling to make ends meet when she lands the job working for Tate as his assistant.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424784i/847040.jpg" width="266" height="355" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>The sexual tension in this book is so freaking thick you could cut it with a knife.</strong><br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424784ra/847041.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper finds herself being pulled in by all that is Tate Larson. He has moments where a softhearted and gentle man shine through and Piper is intrigued. But Tate is on an emotional roller coaster ride and he is all over the place.<br><br>Tate wants Piper, then he doesn't want Piper, then he doesn't want Piper with anyone else, then he doesn't want Piper, then he wants Piper, then....<br><br>Tate, make up your freaking mind what you want!<br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424784ra/847042.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tate seriously....<br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400084ra/774923.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em>"Would it be too much to ask for a blow to the head with a blunt object? She could use a bout of amnesia right now." -Piper</em><br><br>He is lucky he is so damn hot! Tate, I love you. Piper, I am not sure why you put up with him.<br><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424784i/847043.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a hot and steamy read. The first kiss is not a innocent as it sounds. It is dirty and yummy. This is a fast paced angst filled romance that will keep you on the edge of your seat waiting to see that Tate will pull next.<br><br><em>"What he was feeling for Piper wasn't something he could stop. It wasn't something he could take back or cut out or burn to ashes. It was a poison that had entered his bloodstream and ripped it's way through his body and he knew the exact moment that it happened: that first kiss."- Tate</em><br><br>Four Gloriously Mercurial Stars<br><a href="http://johnstohbibliomaniac.files.wordpress.com/2013/05/red_star_4_of_5-5405838cef8c4750ec26237ed6595e7c.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="red_star_4_of_5-5405838cef8c4750ec26237ed6595e7c" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380381565i/738924.png" width="75" height="15" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_622403227" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/622403227" />
    <a title="Sara " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5058304-sara"><img alt="Sara " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1439650883p2/5058304.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/622403227?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara " href="/user/show/5058304-sara">Sara </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=fun">fun</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=girfriend-bonding">girfriend-bonding</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622403227" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6597347392026323587"><b>Rating: 4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I am a person who gets on a genre kick. I find one that I fall in love with and immerse myself in it completely. It’s hard to come out of with my OCD but when a book comes along that takes me out of that genre and has me up until the wee hours of the morning to finish it. I dare say it’s a damn good book. I have said it before; I don’t stay up that late for just any book, even though it’s fun to tease my husband that I am up with another man. Anyway…<br/><br/>That First Kiss was a breath </span>
  <span id="freeText6597347392026323587" style="display:none"><b>Rating: 4.5 stars</b><br /><br />I am a person who gets on a genre kick. I find one that I fall in love with and immerse myself in it completely. It’s hard to come out of with my OCD but when a book comes along that takes me out of that genre and has me up until the wee hours of the morning to finish it. I dare say it’s a damn good book. I have said it before; I don’t stay up that late for just any book, even though it’s fun to tease my husband that I am up with another man. Anyway…<br /><br />That First Kiss was a breath of fresh air. I had the privilege of reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16125520.Stranded__Night_Calls___1_" title="Stranded (Night Calls, #1) by J.C. Valentine" rel="nofollow noopener">Stranded</a>,the novella before this. It’s not needed to read it first but I would recommend it for the simple pleasure of knowing Felix and Poppy’s story and getting to see them once again. <br /><br />So, we meet Piper Donovan as she is being interviewed for a new position, a position that can seriously make or break her current living situation. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So would you say that you work well with others?”<br />Piper nodded enthusiastically. “Oh, yes. I haven’t met a person yet that has been able to get me riled.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />Um, are you sure about that Piper? After landing a position with Bookish Temptations (that name was the only thing that bugged me about this book) Piper goes out with her girl friends to celebrate with one central goal, to get drunk and get laid. I adore that Piper is a <i>WOMAN</i>, she is not some little girl who is unaware or afraid of sex. Piper is an adult, living in a grown up world where she owns her sexuality and if a one night stand is what she wants it is what she is going to get and her friends will make damn sure about that. What else are best girlfriends for than to look after you wants and needs.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Seriously, if you don’t go over there and scoop up that hottie one of us will.” Sheila motioned to herself and the others. “Believe me, if you don’t want him, one of us will be more than willing to take one for the team. Besides, you need to get laid.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />When Piper catches the eye of man across the dance floor she is instantly attracted but with a turn of her head he disappears, sigh, oh well the night must go on. The girls head out to burn off the drinks with a bit of dancing; Piper feels hands on her hips and gets into the bump and grind (come on...a little R. Kelly never hurt anyone, he is still trapped in the closet after all) and upon a spin she comes face to face with HIM! <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The man had two perfect dimples that she had the urge to lick. She didn’t of course, because that would be creepy, but she could do whatever she wanted in her mind, and she was licking his face like it was the last creamsicle on the planet.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />Well now. I do declare! Our feisty Piper heads off for a bit of fun with Mr. Sexy Dimples and ends up with an altering kiss at the end of a little counter action…that first kiss. Oh boy. <br /><br />As Piper heads into work for her first day she is ready to take on the ego inflated author who blows through assistants as fast as Charlie Sheen blows through brain cells. Oh no, say it ain’t so…her new “second boss” the one she has to work side by side closely with is none other than Mr. Sexy Dimples himself, aka Tate Larson. Poor Piper, if it wasn’t bad enough to see a one night stand in the broad daylight to have it be this man? Oh I felt for her, I did. <br /><br />The relationship between Piper and Tate is strained to say the least. He is well, Tate and pretty much an ass and she is Piper just trying to do her best to keep her job and her head above water. What doesn’t help is the sexual tension between these two. Piper wants Tate but won’t give in. Tate wants Piper but won’t give in…they drove me nuts most of the time but had some of the funniest scenes and goodness there were a few instances where I had to kick my foot out of the covers to cool off they got so damn hot. It’s been a while since a standard romance could do that to me. Thank you Ms. Valentine for allowing me to have faith in this genre again, I had thought it long gone. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The problem was – and if she was being completely honest with herself – as much as she detested Tate Larson, she was finding it more and more difficult every day to say no to him. Tate Larson was going to be the death of her, but oh what a way to die.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />Mr. Tate Larson, you are one head strong man with a tongue of gold. Some of the things that come out of your mouth make it justifiable to slap you silly but then you come out with these words, these oh so sexy words that had me melting. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What are you doing?” Piper flattened herself against the door as Tate tilted his head toward her. <br />“Thinking,” he said distracted. <br />“About what?” Her heart pounded and she was finding it harder to breathe. <br />His lips whispered across hers. “Kissing you.” He dragged his lips down the slope of her jaw to her neck. “Tasting you.” When he reached the curve of her shoulder his hand dipped between her legs and cupped her. “Fucking you,” he whispered…</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Um...yeah. What was I saying? Oh yes, Tate and that filthy, deletacable mouth of his. Yeah, that was just one of the reasons I fell for that man. This is one of the others, just one.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Damn, but her smile was fucking gorgeous. Just seeing her smile caused his own to stretch across his face and his worries to disappear as if they had never existed.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br /><br />Watching these two fight their attraction, then give in, then fight it again only to give in AGAIN <i>(ahem - Las Vegas hotel room - just saying.)</i> was a great ride that I would gladly take again. Piper and Tate are a match made in frustrating heaven but seeing them grow in their relationship was so much fun. There really is a match out there for everyone even if they drive you nuts and no, I am not talking about stage five clinger nuts, Sheila. <br /><br /><i>That First Kiss</i> was a fun read, a book you can curl up and get lost in, smile at, gush over, fawn over and route for the couple to finally get it together so they can <b>BE</b> together. I simply adored this story; this boy meets girl have a one night stand and are thrust together by fate. Sounds cliché but the author does a great job of telling a sweet and sexy love story of two stubborn as hell individuals who finally give into what they want. <br /><br /><br /><br /><i>ARC and review copy provided by the author.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6597347392026323587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_654693334" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/654693334" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/654693334?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654693334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11368538423850167762"><b>4.5 Shake. You. Until. You. Shut-up. And. Listen. To. Me. Stars!</b><br/><i>Copy received in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>Tate and Piper's story starts of with one hell of a <b>bang</b>.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427307ra/854182.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Piper is in desperate need of a job in order to avoid having to move back home. But when she lands a job that could be the answers to all her prayers she suddenly realizes that it is the answer to all her nightmares and fantasies as well. Tate is the arrogant, pushy and down-right asshole that can't seem to keep an assistant for a</span>
  <span id="freeText11368538423850167762" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Shake. You. Until. You. Shut-up. And. Listen. To. Me. Stars!</b><br><i>Copy received in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>Tate and Piper's story starts of with one hell of a <b>bang</b>.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427307ra/854182.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper is in desperate need of a job in order to avoid having to move back home. But when she lands a job that could be the answers to all her prayers she suddenly realizes that it is the answer to all her nightmares and fantasies as well. Tate is the arrogant, pushy and down-right asshole that can't seem to keep an assistant for any length of time. A star author at Bookish Temptations in need of a new assistant who is tough enough to put him in his place and put up with his bullshit. But neither of them expected to be face to face in that coffee shop after that explosive night in the club. <br><br>Tate is man that has disconnected the emotions from sex. He has seen first hand how love can break a person. Unwilling to accept that he needs both, he has created a life full of one night stands. And taking a page out of Pretty Woman doesn't turn sex into an intimate moment by allowing himself to expose himself with the act of kissing. But something about this girl makes him want to taste her lips - and that kiss is about to ruin him, he just doesn't realize it yet.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416198ra/821871.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Piper seems to push all of the wrong buttons with Tate; but still able to somehow manage to retain her job lasting longer than the ones before him. But his excessive need for her to be at his beck and call at all hours might just be more about being possessive and less about her job. Their one night has not left their thoughts but this is strictly business. Piper has seen the man in action and although she is desperate to be under him again; she refuses to give in to the sexual chemistry. Tate is not sure why he let her get under his skin and the back and forth angst is frustrating as all hell. There were multiple times that I wanted to throw my Kindle across the room. Frustrating doesn't even begin to explain these two and their lack of ability to communicate. But I am a complete sucker for these angst filled stories that make you want to pull out your hair and put your fist through walls.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397322ra/766529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sexual tension at points in this was off the charts but always seemed to leave you hanging - wanting more. Needing it to go one step further. Needing both of them to just shut up for a minute and let their bodies do the thinking for them. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427307i/854183.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every time you think <i>this is it</i>, that finally someone is going to put on their big-girl panties and admit to what they are feeling the other person opens their big mouth or does something that causes the other to retreat back into their head. The inability to simply communicate and see beyond the fear of getting hurt was enough to drive you insane but completely sucked you into this story. Love - lust - hate all blended together in one fucked up mixing bowl that made you crave to stick your fingers in and lick up every last bit.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412877ra/812240.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the story was nearing the end I had one repeating thought playing through my head...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391945ra/754652.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427307ra/854184.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two were so dysfunctional, they both were so frustrating. But I could not get enough. Romantic? No. Hot? Yes. These two created sparks easily but warm fuzzy feelings were not on the menu. They took the long way to get to the place we all knew they would end up. But it was the right path. Tate was far too complicated and screwed up for it to be easy. Piper to stubborn to take a moment and try to see what was in front of her - what his actions meant; why he did the things he did. Both so unwilling to just give in - both fighting every feeling...every emotion with everything they had. <br><br>I enjoyed the prior novella in this series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16125520.Stranded__Night_Calls___1_" title="Stranded (Night Calls, #1) by J.C. Valentine" rel="nofollow noopener">Stranded</a>, and was not sure what to expect with the second in the series. I was pleasantly surprised. The feel of the way the story was told felt new - you could feel the difference in style that fit these two characters. Sometimes an author's style doesn't shift. The style remains the same in each book no matter what the situation is. Stranded fit Poppy and Felix's encounter and That First Kiss just fit the angst and frustration of Piper and Tate. An amazing job by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6571021.J_C__Valentine" title="J.C. Valentine" rel="nofollow noopener">J.C. Valentine</a> to tell the story with such a way that fit the feel of the characters. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11368538423850167762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer628751764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3329722880983802383">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href='http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Craves The Angst</a>.<br/><br/><i>I was kindly provided this eARC from the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>4.5 Sexy, Steamy, Salacious Stars!</i>
</b><br/><b>
  <i>Hold Onto Your Panties Ladies, Tate Is On The Prowl!</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>The Rundown:</i>
</b><br/>Tate is a capricious writer with a trust issues, whose past has taught him those who believe in love, commitment and monogamy are destined to fail. Those things are myths people tell themselves to trap them in a doomed relationship. He’s a total alpha male who </span>
  <span id="freeText3329722880983802383" style="display:none">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href="http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Craves The Angst</a>.<br /><br /><i>I was kindly provided this eARC from the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>4.5 Sexy, Steamy, Salacious Stars!</i>
</b><br /><b>
  <i>Hold Onto Your Panties Ladies, Tate Is On The Prowl!</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>The Rundown:</i>
</b><br />Tate is a capricious writer with a trust issues, whose past has taught him those who believe in love, commitment and monogamy are destined to fail. Those things are myths people tell themselves to trap them in a doomed relationship. He’s a total alpha male who wants what he wants and makes no excuses for his temperamental and turbulent moods. <br /><br />When we meet Tate for the first time, he is out clubbing, on the prowl, like most nights, looking for a quick hook up without complications. Seeing Piper across the dance floor, he’s instantly attracted to the dark haired, curvy beauty with the big brown eyes. She’s not his usual type but there’s just something about her that pulls at something deep inside him. Taking his chances and approaching her on the pulsating dance floor, Tate can’t get enough of her taste, her smell, her feel so without much preamble, he whisks her away to the ladies bathroom where they both have one of the most erotic encounters of their lives. Tate never kisses the girls he hooks up with because its too personal, but when the deed is done, Tate can’t resist kissing Piper’s soft, plump lips just once before leaving her. That one kiss is his undoing.<br /><br /><i>Quote Spotlight...</i><br /><b>
  <i>What he was feeling for Piper wasn’t something he could stop. It wasn’t something he could take back or cut out or burn to ashes. It was a poison that had entered his blood stream and ripped its way through his body and he knew the exact moment it happened: that first kiss.</i>
</b><br /><br />Out on the town with her girlfriends before she starts her new job, Piper can’t believe she just lead herself on a mission of debauchery in the women's bathroom with a guy who’s name she didn't even get. But rebounding from a bad breakup, hooking up is about all she can handle at the moment so she enjoyed the adventure for what it was. When Monday morning arrives and her new job starts, she’s warned that she will be personal assistant to a moody writer who’s run off all his other PA’s. Determined to keep her job and a steady paycheck and not be forced to move back to her childhood home in Alabama, she sets out to find her new charge only to come face to face with her one night stand.<br /> <br />The first thing he does? Fire’s her!<br /><br /><i>Quote Spotlight...</i><br /><b>
  <i>Piper glared at him. Was this guy for real? This was exactly why she preferred one-night stands. When she banged someone in the back room she never has to see their assholian faces again!</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>The Review:</i>
</b><br /><u>That First Kiss (Night Calls #2)</u> is a steamy Adult Contemporary Romance written by <i>J.C.Valentine</i> and though this is the second book in the series, its a stand alone, full length novel.<br /><br />I read the first book in this series, <i>Stranded</i> which was a short/story novella and though I enjoyed it, <b>this book, Completely. Blew. Me. Away!</b> <u>That First Kiss</u> had me laughing, fretting and nervous for our would-be couple. And it had me completely seduced throughout the entire time I was immersed in this incredible read. In short, it was simply amazing!<br /><br />Tate was sexy, steamy, charming, over confidant, completely hilarious at times and a right royal ass at others but his moody temper and his impenetrable walled heart was no match for the irresistible Piper.<br /><br />Piper was strong willed, confident and beautiful. She worked hard, had morals and though she’d been trampled on, she still had hope. I loved her character!<br /><br />Their chemistry was off-the-charts hot and watching these two come together was sinful and fun. <br /><br /><i>Quote Spotlight...</i><br /><b>
  <i>Tate smirked. “Honestly, you make me sound like some sort of caveman. Had that been the case, you would be unconscious and completely at my mercy right now. And trust me,” he said, his voice growing husky as they fell off his tongue and he stepped forward, closing the distance between them. “I can think of so many things to do to you, and you wouldn’t be complaining about any of them.”</i>
</b><br /><br />This book has it all. Steam, fun, angst, fabulous characters and heartfelt emotions. And best of all, there’s no cliffy and there’s a HEA!<br /><br /><i>Quote Spotlight...</i><br /><b>
  <i>“I know I’m an asshole, and I’m sure as hell not worthy of you, but if you give me a chance, I’ll spend the rest of my life trying to be.”</i>
</b> <br /><br />And as an added bonus, we also get to see glimpses of the continuing, developing relationship of Felix and Poppy from the first book, <i>Stranded</i> as Piper and Tate interact with them.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> The Wrap Up:</i>
</b><br />I love how <i>J.C. Valentine</i> writes the best confrontational scenes with entertaining dialogue and hilarious character interactions. I absolutely LOVED, and I do mean LOVED, Tate and Pipers first official meet. Sparks were flying, I was laughing and cringing at the same time, and their laughable and awkward encounter only cemented how much I would adore this crazy ride. And trust me, I wasn’t disappointed. This author has a way with romance, crazy off the wall characters and intense and fun scenes that will captivate your heart and leave you wanting more each time! I can't wait to read the next book in this series. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>More Favorite Quotes and Passages...</i>
</b><br /><i>Tate probably couldn’t see it, but he was this close to being found stuffed in a roadside drainage ditch. - (Piper’s POV)<br /><br /><br />He stayed two steps behind her all the way up to the house, afraid to get too close. It was like he was starring in his own horror movie and had just figured out who the killer was. He had to put on a mask of ignorance and remain calm. As with any psychopath, she could probably smell fear. - (Tate’s POV)<br /><br /><br />His heart was pounding in his chest, a light sheen of sweat had his skin feeling clammy, and if the granny in the Gremlin didn’t get the hell out of his way pronto, he was tempted to roll right over the top of her. - (Tate's POV)<br /><br /><br />“I need to be inside you,” he growled. “I need to feel your naked curves beneath me.” - Tate </i> <br /><br />(Yowza! I need me a Tate ASAP please!)</span>

<div id="review_642327843" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/642327843" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4799984-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386011637p2/4799984.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/642327843?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/4799984-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4799984-anna?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer642327843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11989212749412118669">Piper Donovan is thrilled to land a job that will keep her living in the city she loves and prevent her from having to go back to a life she doesn't want in rural Alabama. While out celebrating her new job with friends she has a very intense encounter with a man she meets at the club. She starts her new job only to realize that the incredibly challenging frustrating man she is now the assistant to is the same man she hooked up with at the club. <br/><br/>Tate is an author who is very demanding and has cau</span>
  <span id="freeText11989212749412118669" style="display:none">Piper Donovan is thrilled to land a job that will keep her living in the city she loves and prevent her from having to go back to a life she doesn't want in rural Alabama. While out celebrating her new job with friends she has a very intense encounter with a man she meets at the club. She starts her new job only to realize that the incredibly challenging frustrating man she is now the assistant to is the same man she hooked up with at the club. <br /><br />Tate is an author who is very demanding and has caused a number of assistants to quit rather than work for someone like him. Piper is able to stand up to him and deal with his moods and demands- but both of them find it difficult to deal with the serious sexual chemistry between them. Both have been hurt in the past, and both struggle to decide how to handle their feelings about one another, which are growing ever more complicated. <br /><br />Based on the author's description of the book, I expected to like it- but I didn't expect it to hook me so quickly or to like it as much as I did. There are elements of the storyline that are familiar to this genre, but the characters felt fresh and there were many elements of the relationships that were unique. I really liked Piper and her girlfriends right from the start. They seem like a lot of fun and obviously create a good support system for each other. Tate was frustrating and screwed up a lot, but it didn't take long for him to hook me too. Piper and Tate had a lot of challenges to face- both personal and professional. Even with the serious chemistry they shared, it wasn't clear how or whether they were going to be able to sort everything out. This was a book that I had a hard time putting down. I found myself thinking about the characters and their situation when I was away from the book. Also- it is funny in a great way. A lot of books I've read lately have seemed a little too aware of how funny they are, and sometimes it seems that the author is trying to hard to be constantly hilarious and it ends up feeling a little fake. The great thing about this book was that a lot of the funny stuff caught me off guard. I would just be reading along, and then all of a sudden one of the characters would totally crack me up. It felt great to experience. <br /><br />This book is the second in a series, but I have not yet read the first. This book can easily be read as a stand-alone. The writing was good, and I will definitely be reading more from this author. <br /><br />*A copy of this book was provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4569634862162955778">This book was crazy hot. Literally from the moment I started it, till the moment I finished it, I was primed and tuned completely into these two characters! Tate is a jackass, but the way he comes full circle is fascinating!   <span id="freeText4569634862162955778" style="display:none">This book was crazy hot. Literally from the moment I started it, till the moment I finished it, I was primed and tuned completely into these two characters! Tate is a jackass, but the way he comes full circle is fascinating! Piper is a bit of a child at times, but she too seems to grow up and mature pretty quickly.<br /><br />Piper needs to find a job fast, she is running out of money quickly and she gets an opportunity that pays well and has some killer perks. Only catch, her boss is a tyrant apparently. She overlooks this and decides to celebrate with her friends. Clubbing is on the agenda and apparently so is a handsome blonde God she meets there. Needless to say, things get hot and heavy and she ends up bumping and grinding with him on and off the dance floor.<br /><br />Tate is a closed off, self absorbed ass who happens to be the man Piper got busy with in the club's bathroom. Things are immediately tense between them and Tate fires her. Literally fires her within minutes of her meeting him. Nice guy right? Turns out, he kinda is. He has had his heartbroken badly and he shuts out any human contact from the opposite sex. If it isn't about sex, he isn't interested in getting to know you. But Piper is under his skin.<br /><br />This book has some funny moments and moments that make you want to cry. It was the first book in a long time where the ex in someone's life wasn't a complete nightmare who was out to break them up. She is actually super sweet and kinda funny. I really enjoyed seeing that, it was a refreshing take on it. We see Piper get close to another man named Tom, who is apparently dreamy as well, and yet she doesn't hurt him. She lets him go and he falls for her friend instead. <br /><br />It was nice to read a book where the tension was based on love and a small misunderstanding vs lust and life and death situations. I enjoyed this book immensely! Did I mention this book was HOT? Because it was ridiculously hot....=)<br /><br />I give it 4.5 lipsticks! You need to buy this one. It's a nice pallet cleanser for those of you who like Crossfire and 50 Shades kind of drama.<br /><br />~B~</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10291309024357574810">Oh my! This book almost immediately heats up. A great book written by one of my new favorite authors!<br/><br/>J.C Valentine tears up the sheets with this book! With the utterly charming, headstrong, determined Piper and the demanding, cold, sexy Tate the characters are a quite the match. It’s interesting to see their characters develop a relationship no matter how hard they try fighting it. Well, Piper does anyway. Piper is determined not to screw up her new job, she doesn’t want to land back in small to</span>
  <span id="freeText10291309024357574810" style="display:none">Oh my! This book almost immediately heats up. A great book written by one of my new favorite authors!<br /><br />J.C Valentine tears up the sheets with this book! With the utterly charming, headstrong, determined Piper and the demanding, cold, sexy Tate the characters are a quite the match. It’s interesting to see their characters develop a relationship no matter how hard they try fighting it. Well, Piper does anyway. Piper is determined not to screw up her new job, she doesn’t want to land back in small town Alabama. But what can you do when your new boss is your one night stand you have been having fantasies about since that night?<br /><br />I have to agree with some of the previous reviews that I have read online about The First Kiss, the bathroom scene is undoubtedly one of the best in the book. The author burned the pages with that one! But this book is so much more than that. A chance at true love when the odds and the past are stacked against you. Just how hard would you fight when you never wanted to put yourself in the position of caring for someone ever again? I think everyone can relate to the mindset, I think we have all been hurt that bad by someone we cared for.<br /><br />If you have read the first book in the Night Calls series, Stranded, you will be happy to see Poppy and Felix make appearances in That First Kiss. Which thrilled me to pieces. Not only do I like the characters Poppy and Felix, Poppy by herself has a charismatic draw that readers will love. It is nice to see the ‘after’. Felix was a dynamic character in Stranded and it was awesome to see him cast as Tate Larson’s boss and close friend in this book.<br /><br />This book has been hotter than the weather in Cleveland and honestly burns the pages up! Get your copy NOW!</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8806422789044847600">this story has been done before. The heroine meets a hot guy in a bar right before she starts a new job and bangs him (this time in a bathroom and yes, the sex is hot!). When she goes to work, oops! The hot guy is her boss. It's not a new story, but JC Valentine did it really well! <br/><br/>Tate is an asshole with a capital A. Honestly, I was never really sure that I liked him. Especially the way he treated my lovely Thomas. I loved him! He redeemed himself in the end, but it was a rough ride! <br/><br/>Piper is t</span>
  <span id="freeText8806422789044847600" style="display:none">this story has been done before. The heroine meets a hot guy in a bar right before she starts a new job and bangs him (this time in a bathroom and yes, the sex is hot!). When she goes to work, oops! The hot guy is her boss. It's not a new story, but JC Valentine did it really well! <br /><br />Tate is an asshole with a capital A. Honestly, I was never really sure that I liked him. Especially the way he treated my lovely Thomas. I loved him! He redeemed himself in the end, but it was a rough ride! <br /><br />Piper is the latest in a long line of assistants for Tate. He goes through them like beer in a frat house. He treats them all like crap and they all end up lasting for 15 minutes with him. Piper is different. She stands up to his crap, gives it back and refuses to let him fire her. I love her spunk! <br /><br />Let's discuss the tension in this book. It was THICK. There was a looooooong period of the book that was just buildup to an explosion. It was really well done. I was getting a bit hot under the collar myself for a while. <br /><br />My favorite parts of this book were actually the girlfriend interactions. Piper has AMAZING friends and their banter was just awesome. I loved it!! I am hoping that Thomas gets a book with a certain friend of Piper's who I just adore! <br /><br />Bottom line time: If you love a story about an jerk getting redemption, you will love this one. I personally did enjoy it, and in the end Tate and Piper made sense...but I still wanted to kick him in the family jewels a LOT. </span>

    <a title="BBMoreB ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4948179-bbmoreb"><img alt="BBMoreB ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389184673p2/4948179.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/679674206?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BBMoreB ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="BBMoreB ~" href="/user/show/4948179-bbmoreb">BBMoreB ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 1230000139561" href="/book/show/18043696-that-first-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4948179-bbmoreb?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679674206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11065824402970641618">This author’s writing style is descriptive, adventurous and enlightening. Her ability to create and portray characters with realistic reactions is unblemished. This well-paced story can change direction in an instant without leaving the reader feeling lost. She allows the characters emotions to naturally progress the story – often exposing their vulnerabilities. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>Only now she was stuck in a darkened corner while her boss and former one-night stand tried to hook up with anything with a pussy.</blockquote>
</b><b>
</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11065824402970641618" style="display:none">This author’s writing style is descriptive, adventurous and enlightening. Her ability to create and portray characters with realistic reactions is unblemished. This well-paced story can change direction in an instant without leaving the reader feeling lost. She allows the characters emotions to naturally progress the story – often exposing their vulnerabilities. <br /><b>
  <blockquote>Only now she was stuck in a darkened corner while her boss and former one-night stand tried to hook up with anything with a pussy.</blockquote>
</b><b>
  <blockquote>“I just know I woke up half-dressed and in my boss’s bed” – Piper to Sheila</blockquote>
</b><br />She developed an all inclusive world with an incredible supporting cast that provides the prefect background to sustain the overall realism. Not to mention the smoking-hot sex scenes…this author has mastered the erotic romance. Everything is well-balanced! <b>
  <u>Highly Recommended!</u>
</b><br /><br /><i>Disclosure: This ebook was provided to me free of charge for the sole purpose of an honest review. All thoughts, comments, and ratings are my own.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12903441184204626502"><i>I received a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review </i><br/><br/>Verdict: 4 scorching stars!<br/><br/><i>"A person could have sex with any number of random people and have it remain a completely superficial function of life, but the moment they chose to seal their lips with another, the soul deep, heart afflicting connection would be made and there would be no turning back."</i> -Tate Larson<br/><br/>I chose to read & review this book because it seemed a perfect candidate to feed my growing addiction for hot assholian boss</span>
  <span id="freeText12903441184204626502" style="display:none"><i>I received a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review </i><br><br>Verdict: 4 scorching stars!<br><br><i>"A person could have sex with any number of random people and have it remain a completely superficial function of life, but the moment they chose to seal their lips with another, the soul deep, heart afflicting connection would be made and there would be no turning back."</i> -Tate Larson<br><br>I chose to read &amp; review this book because it seemed a perfect candidate to feed my growing addiction for hot assholian bosses. I figured if the dynamic was anything like that between Chloe Mills and Bennett Ryan in <i>Beautiful Bastard</i>, I was game. OMG, did it not disappoint! Once I started reading, I found it extremely difficult to put down! <br><br>Piper Donovan is a struggling twenty-something year old whose biggest fear is failure. She knows that failure means having to go back to her hometown in Alabama. Something she's worked hard to avoid. Unemployed and desperate, she finally gets a break when she lands the personal assistant position to Tate Larson; an incredibly difficult and gorgeous star author at Bookish Temptations. <br><br>*SPOILER ALERT* <br><br>Blissfully ignorant to the impending doom that awaits, she decides to celebrate her new job with a girls night out. There, she is drawn to an incredibly sexy man who lures her into none other than the ladies room and proceeds to bang the heck out of her. Parting ways without so much as catching his name, Piper's thoughts become inundated by reveries of the beautiful stranger. She can't seem to nor does she want to forget the feel of his lips during that stolen kiss. <br><br>On her first day of work, Piper is sent to a coffee shop to meet up with her boss...and gets a lot more than she bargained for. Spotted...hot guy from the club staring straight at her! Walking over, she makes small talk only to come to the horrid realization that he's her new boss. What happens next you ask? He fires her! That sets the tone for this deliciously hilarious tale of lust, love &amp; unadulterated loathing. <br><br>Tate Larson is a brilliant writer and demanding slave driver to his personal assistants. So much so, he can't seem to hold on to one for any long period of time. Nobody has been able to put up with his bs until now. Enter Piper, Tate monopolizes her time to the extent where she even acts as his DD when he takes his hot man-whore self clubbing. Determined to keep a steady job, she takes everything Tate dishes...including the major cock-blocking he constantly unleashes on her. Enter Tomas, a sexy gentleman who totally wants in Piper's panties. Little does he know, Tate Larson happens to be the gatekeeper. Let the cock-blocking begin! <br><br>The mayhem that unfolds is throughly entertaining. The sexual tension that ensues is both infuriating and addicting. Neither Piper nor Tate could forget sizzling first encounter sealed with that amazing first kiss. Nonetheless, they were determined to keep their relationship professional. But there's only so much angst a person can handle. After some major brooding, Tate finally embraces his true feelings for Piper...not just as his coffee girl. The rest is the stuff of rainbows and unicorns, my favorite part! After a roller coaster of sexual tension you're strapped into, we get the sweetest ending...and all is well in book boyfriend land. <br><br>I really enjoyed the intense relationship dynamic between Tate and Piper. The author did an amazing job of capturing the reader's attention and never letting them go. Hooray for smokin' hot assholes who turn into smokin' hot lovable assholes! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380756565ra/3120116.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380438067ra/885509.gif" alt="some_text" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First time they met – it was a total explosion. Contrary to the pics – the first time they did it wasn’t traditional. It was on a bar – it was hot, dirty, mindless sex. They didn’t share names, address or trade numbers. After they were done, they went into their separate ways, pretending it was nothing.<br><br>The act had consumed their thoughts more than they would have wanted. They thought it was the last time they were going to see each other, but they were in for a big surprise came in Monday morning when Piper Donovan walked in on Tate Larson as his new assistant.<br><br>Tate Larson didn’t believed in relationship, after the men in his family had failed. He believed that failing in relationships is in their genes. He tried once – falling in love. But after his ex-girlfriend cheated on him, he decided to stick to the less complicated: one-night stand: no strings, no commitments, no names. That is until Piper came into his life. In fairness to him – no matter how much his love life or relationship status is in chaos, he is focused on his work.<br><br>Piper is in need of the job, so when she lands a position at Bookish Temptations, she owed her to herself to celebrate. With her friends, she decided to go out, dance a little, drink a lot and perhaps hook up a bit. What she didn’t expect was to run into Tate Larson, had him bend her over and gave her the most amazing orgasm in her life in somewhere she least expected. Yay. How can she possibly work with him?! But when bills are piling up, and leases are due, she needed to pull her big-girl panties up and be professional. Only that, the Tate that she knew that evening and the Tate she’s working with now are totally two different people. He’s an ultimate pain in the a** who makes her life miserable daily.<br><br>The attraction is strong, and both of them is struggling to maintain professionalism in the workplace. But sometimes gravity pulls to hard, and it’s simpler to just fall in rather than to fight it.<br><br>THAT FIRST KISS is a rollercoaster ride. Their chemistry is off the charts, I wonder why my Kindle isn’t burning up yet. These two is totally into each other, but because of work, past issues and insecurities – they tend to assume the worse. I love the characters, especially Tate’s mom and Sheila. I didn’t expect to like Tom and Casey too! I thought I’d want to rip them out from the story, but as it goes on, you won’t have a choice but love them as well. The couple are frustrating, but you will adore them just as much. This was one heck of a ride I totally enjoyed. <br><br><i>*ARC Copy was given in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

  <span id="freeText3789786030658842961" style="display:none">ARC courtesy of the author and publicist for honest review.<br /><br />Great book difficult to put down. Thank you Ms Valentine for the arc of this book and I can not wait to see the next one you have in store for the readers!<br /><br />Ms Valentine , gives us two incredible strong willed, opinionated , driven characters whose interaction together is incredible and sexually charged!<br /><br />The story line opens on Piper Donavan, a young women who has moved to the big city from small town Alabama to escape small town life and a medelsom mother. Piper's new life however is in jeopardy without employment and out of desperation she applies for a job with a publishing house Bookish Times as a personal assistant to an author and luckily gets it! Acquiring employment demands a night out with the BFF 's drinking, dancing and prowling, which Piper turns out to be very successful at, soon she finds herself on the dance floor with one incredibly handsome man and then even sooner in a locked ladies room with said sexy man( and anything I would write at this point would not do tha scene justice). But one important piece hot guy breaks down and kisses her and makes the whole interlude personal! <br /><br />For Piper , first day of her new job arrives all to soon and to her dismay her new boss Tate Larsen her sexy, hard nosed difficult to work with boss is no other than the hottie from the club ladies room. <br />Tate, has spent years moving from one unknown hook up to the next not wanting to forge any bonds and for him Karma is a bitch since he made the tragic error of kissing her and making it personal he has not been able to get Piper out of his mind; to top all she is his new employee. Tate has had his fill of bad relationships and has vowed never again.<br />Pipers last relationship was no better, both are skittish and vulnerable but Suprisingly for me I thought Tate to be the more vulnerable.<br />The remainder of the book is spent with these two doing a classic push away and pull you back, with incredibly hot sex scences, warm romantic scenes and the Oh my God , just shoot him and put poor Piper out of her misery scenes.<br /><br />I have given away more than enough plot line but there is so much more , if you like contemporary romance add this to your Tbr list. <br /><br />I will state it again great book , I loved it!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText8836717726046961339" style="display:none">***RRC provided in exchange for an honest review***<br /><br />Wow! Such a combination of emotions!! <br />I loved that this wasn't the normal romance story. It had a depth that I truly loved. <br />Starting with a BANG! ( quite literally!) and it didn't stop. I loved Tate and I hated him, but overall I believed him, and I think that really says something for the authors ability to weave this beautiful story! <br />My only wish, is that he got his crap together sooner! But boy oh boy when he put the charm on *swoon*<br /><br />"What are you doing?" Piper flattened herself against the door as Tate tilted his head toward her. <br />"Thinking,"he said distracted. <br />"About what?" When he reached the curve of her shoulder his hand dipped between her legs and cupped her. As with any psychopath, she could probably smell fear."<br /><br />Piper was such a STRONG female lead, which is SUCH a nice change from almost every other romance novel I've read of late. <br />I enjoyed her sense of humour a lot! <br /><br />"The man had two perfect dimples that she had the urge to lick. She didn’t of course, because that would be creepy, but she could do whatever she wanted in her mind, and she was licking his face like it was the last creamsicle on the planet."<br /><br />I loved that he straight up fired her in the first minute!! I will say I felt bad for Pipers secondary love interest Tom!<br /><br />Overall I really enjoyed reading their story :)<br /><br />This is the first book I have read from this author, however it's certainly wont be the last. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3258034822649841593"><b>This is the story of Tate and Piper, who meet at a night-club, share a quickie & a poignant kiss in a public bathroom, and then go their separate ways. <i>Or not</i></b>.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427281i/854143._SY540_.jpg' width='200' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It turns out that Tate is Piper’s new boss, and the following Monday they officially “meet” for the first time.<br/><br/>The story is less angsty than I had expected. Some parts are very funny and Piper’s friend Sheila is a hoot. Tate starts off being a jerk, and for most of the book I seriously wondered what Piper possibly liked about him (besides</span>
  <span id="freeText3258034822649841593" style="display:none"><b>This is the story of Tate and Piper, who meet at a night-club, share a quickie &amp; a poignant kiss in a public bathroom, and then go their separate ways. <i>Or not</i></b>.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427281i/854143._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It turns out that Tate is Piper’s new boss, and the following Monday they officially “meet” for the first time.<br><br>The story is less angsty than I had expected. Some parts are very funny and Piper’s friend Sheila is a hoot. Tate starts off being a jerk, and for most of the book I seriously wondered what Piper possibly liked about him (besides the sex in the bathroom), especially when another gorgeous, <i>nice</i> suitor appears. Tate is absolutely horrible to her and to everyone else. His previous assistants have all quit, and Piper takes all his crap. Thankfully, Tate is redeemed on time and I found myself cheering for them to move past numerous misunderstandings. <br><br>The book moves quickly at times and then slows down in others, but it never lost my attention or interest. It was also less erotic than I expected, which is good because the sex scenes served to develop the romance and not just to fill the pages. It is still a very steamy story though. Great ending and epilogue, I would definitely read the next book.<br><br><i>ARC received from author in exchange for an honest review</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676422542" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15112646259316378903">This was a very captivating novel that revolves around a will they/won’t they relationship. Valentine pulled me in right from the very beginning and didn’t let me go until the fat lady sang. <br/><br/>Valentine is the type of writer who can pick any situation and make you see the possibilities behind it. Although a very descriptive writer, she uses each word towards a greater goal. Nothing is wasted on irrelevant details and everything combines for a seamless whole. The world that she has created with thi</span>
  <span id="freeText15112646259316378903" style="display:none">This was a very captivating novel that revolves around a will they/won’t they relationship. Valentine pulled me in right from the very beginning and didn’t let me go until the fat lady sang. <br /><br />Valentine is the type of writer who can pick any situation and make you see the possibilities behind it. Although a very descriptive writer, she uses each word towards a greater goal. Nothing is wasted on irrelevant details and everything combines for a seamless whole. The world that she has created with this novel is so fully developed that you feel like you’ve lived there with the characters. <br /><br />The characters in this novel are phenomenal. They are real and have real hurts and fears. As a reader you find yourself loving and hating them in equal measure. And it’s not just the main characters that are well developed. Each and every person who graces these pages is someone that you get to know. I love how Valentine worked the characters from the 1st Night Calls novel into this book without overpowering the new lead characters. It adds a sense of continuity to the series. <br /><br />Overall, this novel was an amazing follow-up to the 1st Night Calls novel. Valentine has me hooked and I can’t wait to read more. This is definitely one author who, no matter what genre she writes, always keeps me captivated. Each novel leaves me anxiously awaiting the next. <br /><br />Please note that I received this novel free of charge from the author in exchange for an honest review.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5442774307147162785">Arrogant author and playboy Tate Larson, has a love them and leave them approach. He feeds of the attraction and makes sure each woman is left with pleasure, but he has a hard and fast rule, never kiss them.   <span id="freeText5442774307147162785" style="display:none">Arrogant author and playboy Tate Larson, has a love them and leave them approach. He feeds of the attraction and makes sure each woman is left with pleasure, but he has a hard and fast rule, never kiss them. Seeing Piper Donovan in the club, Tate is caught off guard, she is easily the most beautiful woman he has ever seen. He wants a touch, just a moment, but he is unprepared for the passionate, if brief, sexual encounter they share which ends in a kiss.<br /><br />Imagine the look on Tate's face when he meets his new assistant, none other than the beauty who has haunted his thoughts since their encounter. He tries to fire her, he gets flipped off. He acts as his usual surly self trying to chase his latest assistant away, she is not impressed and has no problem voicing her opinions about his behavior. Tate knows he is in trouble, he is falling hard for Piper which he vowed never to do again. Despite all that and with as much class as broken down jalopy, Tate tries to show Piper how he really feels and ends up chasing away the best thing that has every happened to him.<br /><br />Witty, laugh out loud humor. I loved Piper, she is tough cookie and I absolutely loved Tate, even when he was a jerk. The two together are walking mixed signals, which is the perfect blend for an outstanding story.</span>

I loved Pipers personality and Tate's awesomeness. They were hilarious sweet and so darn sexy. I highly recommend this sweet read for.some laughs and a whole lot of lovin.<br /><br />**Wrote this on my phone and so my review was Sooo short! Wanted to add a bit more. The way these two meet is out of sight HOT HOT HOT. I mean who could EVER go to a club bathroom again. I adored the back and forth dialogue between these two. Piper learned NOT to take a thing off of Tate and he was thrown off his game by her not being cowed by him! He was hilarious at times and so darn sexy. <br /><br />I really hate sometimes when another guy is thrown into the mix and he is such a GOOD guy. Tom was like that and I wanted him to find that "special someone" also. <br /><br />The casino scene was hilarious! And then Tate realizes he really screwed up. He goes and gets his girl and we have a great epilogue, wrapping it all up nicely!<br /><br />Just a fun read! Loved it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16630321422520917308" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm so pleased that J.C. kept her promise to write full length books following the juicy hot novella <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16125520.Stranded__Night_Calls___1_' title='Stranded (Night Calls, #1) by J.C.   <span id="freeText5374337647811815820" style="display:none"><b>4.5 smoldering, moody Alpha packed stars!</b><br /><br />God I love a moody, angsty, Alpha male and Tate is exactly that!<br />I also love a feisty, no-shit type of heroine and Pippa fits the bill.<br /><br />The series is developing nicely. I'm so pleased that J.C. kept her promise to write full length books following the juicy hot novella <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16125520.Stranded__Night_Calls___1_" title="Stranded (Night Calls, #1) by J.C. Valentine" rel="nofollow noopener">Stranded</a>(which I loved).<br /><br />The books are companion reads with no cliffy to worry about. <br />Poppy and Felix from book one fit smoothly into this one and the story has a good flow. <br /><br />I read it in a day and half, sometimes we need feel good books along with our trawl for hot sex! And you do get both with the Night Calls series. That bathroom scene at the beginning was absofuckinglutely yummy! <br /><br />ARC kindly offered to me by the publishers - Thank you - loved it!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4904568496213562141">WOW! This is my first time reading this author and I have to say that I am blown away. This book was amazing! J.C. Valentine has written a fantastic book that kept my attention throughout the entire read. The storyline and character growth were perfect. Piper and Tate were great characters. Piper was the ever efficient assistant and Tate was the emotionally eccentric author. One would think that the “boss and his assistant” storyline has been written many times but not this way. This was differe</span>
  <span id="freeText4904568496213562141" style="display:none">WOW! This is my first time reading this author and I have to say that I am blown away. This book was amazing! J.C. Valentine has written a fantastic book that kept my attention throughout the entire read. The storyline and character growth were perfect. Piper and Tate were great characters. Piper was the ever efficient assistant and Tate was the emotionally eccentric author. One would think that the “boss and his assistant” storyline has been written many times but not this way. This was different and very creative. Oh and wait till you meet Thomas ;) Their story was fantastic and I will definitely be watching out for whatever this author writes next!<br /><br />**ARC provided for honest review**<br />for more reviews visit welovekink (dot) com</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('O4C467Atx7KE9GAtwzh+m+kdOEvhFXkGNGgmsrLtyRraFy00OLFi+bfMtfrF9dMBPG2BbfOAgBINkV1Ewjvihg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bqbZLKes35SFI4b904GBu+JWCvuZVj63hZXEFIDuEIKPMUzzLzB637YbUyrVTCwhNyaz3YvDx6O8bL/i8Dg7Hg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer15864531075126270802">J.C. Valentine is the USA Today and International bestselling author of the Night Calls and Wayward Fighters Series and the Forbidden Trilogy. Her vivid imagination and love of words and romance had her penning her own romance stories from an early age, which, despite being poorly edited and written longhand, she forced friends and family members to read. No, she isn't sorry.<br/><br/>J.C. lives in the Nort</span>
  <span id="freeText15864531075126270802" style="display:none">J.C. Valentine is the USA Today and International bestselling author of the Night Calls and Wayward Fighters Series and the Forbidden Trilogy. Her vivid imagination and love of words and romance had her penning her own romance stories from an early age, which, despite being poorly edited and written longhand, she forced friends and family members to read. No, she isn't sorry.<br /><br />J.C. lives in the Northwest with her three amazing children and far too many pets, and together they spend much of their free time enjoying movies or the outdoors. Among the many hats she wears, J.C. is an entrepreneur. Having graduated with honors, she holds a Bachelor's in English and when she isn't writing, you can find her editing for fellow authors.<br /><br /><br />Sign up for J.C.'s newsletter and never miss a thing! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1KxXWWB">http://bit.ly/1KxXWWB</a><br /><br />Connect with JC on Facebook! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/JCValetineAuthor">http://www.facebook.com/JCValetineAuthor</a></span>
